Th\u1ebf chi\u1ebfn th\u1ee9 nh\u1ea5t n\u1ed5 ra, Keynes l\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c trong B\u1ed9 T\u00e0i ch\u00ednh. V\u00e0 khi Hi\u1ec7p \u01b0\u1edbc h\u00f2a b\u00ecnh Versailles \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c k\u00fd k\u1ebft, \u00f4ng xu\u1ea5t b\u1ea3n cu\u1ed1n \u201cNh\u1eefng h\u1ec7 qu\u1ea3 kinh t\u1ebf c\u1ee7a H\u00f2a b\u00ecnh\u201d (The Economic Consequences of the Peace). Trong t\u00e1c ph\u1ea9m n\u00e0y \u00f4ng ch\u1ec9 tr\u00edch vi\u1ec7c \u0111\u00f2i h\u1ecfi kho\u1ea3n b\u1ed3i th\u01b0\u1eddng chi\u1ebfn tranh qu\u00e1 cao t\u1eeb m\u1ed9t n\u01b0\u1edbc \u0110\u1ee9c b\u1ea1i tr\u1eadn v\u00e0 d\u1ef1 \u0111o\u00e1n r\u1eb1ng \u0111i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y s\u1ebd l\u00e0m t\u0103ng kh\u00e1t v\u1ecdng tr\u1ea3 th\u00f9 c\u1ee7a ng\u01b0\u1eddi \u0110\u1ee9c. Cu\u1ed1n s\u00e1ch b\u00e1n ch\u1ea1y v\u00e0 khi\u1ebfn \u00f4ng tr\u1edf n\u00ean n\u1ed5i ti\u1ebfng tr\u00ean to\u00e0n th\u1ebf gi\u1edbi.\n- Trong nh\u1eefng n\u0103m gi\u1eefa hai cu\u1ed9c chi\u1ebfn, Keynes t\u00edch l\u0169y \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c m\u1ed9t kho\u1ea3n l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn c\u00e1 nh\u00e2n \u0111\u00e1ng k\u1ec3 t\u1eeb th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng t\u00e0i ch\u00ednh. V\u00e0 v\u1edbi t\u01b0 c\u00e1ch l\u00e0 ng\u01b0\u1eddi qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd t\u00e0i ch\u00ednh c\u1ee7a tr\u01b0\u1eddng King\u2019s College, \u00f4ng \u0111\u00e3 gi\u00fap c\u1ea3i thi\u1ec7n \u0111\u00e1ng k\u1ec3 t\u00ecnh h\u00ecnh t\u00e0i ch\u00ednh c\u1ee7a tr\u01b0\u1eddng.\n- N\u0103m 1926, \u00f4ng k\u1ebft h\u00f4n v\u1edbi Lydia Lopokova, m\u1ed9t v\u0169 c\u00f4ng ballet ng\u01b0\u1eddi Nga. \nT\u00e1c ph\u1ea9m n\u1ed5i ti\u1ebfng nh\u1ea5t c\u1ee7a Keynes \u2013 cu\u1ed1n \u201cL\u00fd thuy\u1ebft chung v\u1ec1 Vi\u1ec7c l\u00e0m, L\u00e3i su\u1ea5t v\u00e0 Ti\u1ec1n t\u1ec7\u201d (The General Theory of Employment, Interest and Money) \u2013 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c xu\u1ea5t b\u1ea3n n\u0103m 1936 v\u00e0 tr\u1edf th\u00e0nh chu\u1ea9n m\u1ef1c cho c\u00e1c t\u01b0 t\u01b0\u1edfng kinh t\u1ebf v\u1ec1 sau. Khi Th\u1ebf chi\u1ebfn th\u1ee9 hai n\u1ed5 ra, \u00f4ng l\u1ea1i l\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c cho B\u1ed9 T\u00e0i ch\u00ednh. The concept of \"Power of 3\" signifies that market makers' algorithms perform three essential actions related to price on each trading day.\n\nThese three actions are categorized as Accumulation, Manipulation, and Distribution, often abbreviated as AMD:\n\nAccumulation: In this phase, market makers gather liquidity by creating a ranging market. The purpose of establishing a ranging market is to entice both buyers and sellers to enter the market, believing that the price will move in their favor.\n\nManipulation: Following the accumulation of both buying and selling orders, market makers manipulate the market to attract another group of traders known as breakout traders. However, this manipulation is not their intended direction for the day. It is merely a tactic to increase liquidity. This increased liquidity then guides them to their next step, which is moving and distributing the price according to their actual plan for the day.\n\nDistribution: After manipulating the price in a specific direction different from their initial plan, market makers then distribute the price in their originally intended direction. For instance, if their intention is to buy, they will initially sell in the market and subsequently purchase at a discounted price level.\n\n*Pictures 1: The Theory of ICT Po3\n\n*Pictures 2: Examples of the application of ICT Po3 on the BTC/USDT price chart \n\nLet's look forward to \"PART II: Applications of ICT Power of 3.\"\n\n#Bitcoin #USDT #Crypto #cryptocurrency #Po3 #ICTPo3 #midnightclub #Powerof3", "replyCount": 61, "retweetCount": 0, "likeCount": 55, "quoteCount": 0, "conversationId": 1710606173324656902, "hashtags": [], "cashtags": [], "mentionedUsers": [], "links": [], "viewCount": 441, "retweetedTweet": null, "quotedTweet": null, "place": null, "coordinates": null, "inReplyToTweetId": null, "inReplyToUser": null, "source": "<a href=\"https://mobile.twitter.com\" rel=\"nofollow\">Twitter Web App</a>", "sourceUrl": "https://mobile.twitter.com", "sourceLabel": "Twitter Web App", "media": {"photos": [{"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F71J9oNaIAAK7IX.png"}, {"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F71J_B_aYAAk6DI.png"}], "videos": [], "animated": []}, "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.Tweet"}

V\u1eady 3 s\u1ed1 n\u00e0y \u1ea9n ch\u1ee9a nh\u1eefng b\u00ed m\u1eadt n\u00e0o, c\u00f3 ph\u1ea3i n\u00f3 \u0111\u00e3 gi\u00fap \u00f4ng tr\u1edf th\u00e0nh nh\u00e0 thi\u00ean t\u00e0i l\u1ed7i l\u1ea1c kh\u00f4ng .    \ud83c\udf1fN\u1ed7i \u00e1m \u1ea3nh 3, 6, 9 c\u1ee7a Tesla b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u t\u1eeb vi\u1ec7c \u00f4ng c\u1ed1 \u0111\u1ecbnh con s\u1ed1 3 - v\u00e0 g\u1ee3i \u00fd r\u1eb1ng 3, 6 v\u00e0 9 c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 n\u1eafm gi\u1eef ch\u00eca kh\u00f3a c\u1ee7a v\u0169 tr\u1ee5. Nh\u01b0ng mu\u1ed1n hi\u1ec3u \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u00fd thuy\u1ebft n\u00e0y th\u00ec \u0111\u1ea7u ti\u00ean ch\u00fang ta ph\u1ea3i hi\u1ec3u ch\u00ednh Nikola Tesla tr\u01b0\u1edbc \u0111\u00e3.\n  \ud83c\udf1fNikola Tesla sinh ng\u00e0y 10 th\u00e1ng 7 n\u0103m 1856, l\u00e0 ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00e2n t\u1ed9c Serb \u1edf Croatia ng\u00e0y nay.
